SAMPLE     All the targets were self-supporting foils of          C2165  1   10

           more than 95% for all targets.                         C2165  1   12 
PART-DET   (P)                                                    C2165  1   13 
DETECTOR   (SOLST) A solid-state surface-barrier counter,         C2165  1   14 
           sufficiently deep to stop 11 MeV protons; the energy   C2165  1   15 
           resolution was about 40 keV full width at half-        C2165  1   16 
           maximum.                                               C2165  1   17 
METHOD     (PHD) The 11.0-MeV proton beam was obtained from the   C2165  1   18 
           ORNL Tandem Van de Graaff. Pulse-height spectra of     C2165  1   19 
           the scattered charged particles were obtained at       C2165  1   20 
           5-deg intervals between laboratory angles of 20 and    C2165  1   21 
           165 deg.                                               C2165  1   22 
ERR-ANALYS (DATA-ERR) The relative error, delta sigma, is an      C2165  1   23 
           estimate of error affecting primarily the shapes of    C2165  1   24 
           the angular distributions. For elastic scattering the  C2165  1   25 
           errors due to counting statistics were very small,     C2165  1   26 
           and the estimate of delta sigma was obtained from the  C2165  1   27 
           reproducibility of the data points (relative errors    C2165  1   28 
           to be less than 5% for angles greater than 30          C2165  1   29 
           degrees). For inelastic scattering the major           C2165  1   30 
           contributions to delta sigma include counting          C2165  1   31 
           statistics and the estimation of the error associated  C2165  1   32 
           with subtraction of the background due to the          C2165  1   33 
           low-energy tail of the elastically scattered protons.  C2165  1   34
